## Overview 

The primary purpose of this chapter is to prove that substitution
commutes with itself. Barendgredt (1984) refers to this
as the substitution lemma:
  
    M [x:=N] [y:=L] = M [y:=L] [x:= N[y:=L] ]

In our setting, with de Bruijn indices for variables, the statement of
the lemma becomes:

    M [ N ] [ L ] ≡  M〔 L 〕[ N [ L ] ]                     (substitution)

where the notation `M 〔 L 〕` is for subsituting L for index 1 inside
M.  In addition, because we define substitution in terms of parallel
substitution, we have the following generalization, replacing the
substitution of L with an arbitrary parallel substitution σ.

    subst σ (M [ N ]) ≡ (subst (exts σ) M) [ subst σ N ]    (subst-commute)

The special case for renamings is also useful.

    rename ρ (M [ N ]) ≡ (rename (ext ρ) M) [ rename ρ N ]
                                                     (rename-subst-commute)

The secondary purpose of this chapter is to define the σ algebra of
parallel substitution due to Abadi, Cardelli, Curien, and Levy
(1991). The equations of this algebra not only help us prove the
substitution lemma, but they are generally useful. Futhermore, when
the equations are applied from left to right, they form a rewrite
system that _decides_ whether any two substitutions are equal.

We use the following more succinct notation the `subst` function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⟪_⟫"></a><a id="2076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪_⟫</a> <a id="2080" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2082" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="2084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2084" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2086" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2086" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="2088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2088" class="Bound">A</a><a id="2089" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2091" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2093" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="2099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2084" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2101" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2086" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="2103" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2084" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="2109" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2088" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2111" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2086" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="2115" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="2117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2088" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="2119" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="2121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2121" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="2123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="2125" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2127" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="2129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2129" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="2131" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2133" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6931" class="Function">subst</a> <a id="2139" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2121" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="2141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2129" class="Bound">M</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## The σ algebra of substitution

Substitutions map de Bruijn indices (natural numbers) to terms, so we
can view a substitution simply as a sequence of terms, or more
precisely, as an infinite sequence of terms. The σ algebra consists of
four operations for building such sequences: identity `ids`, shift
`↑`, cons `M • σ`, and sequencing `σ ⨟ τ`.  The sequence `0, 1, 2, ...`
is constructed by the identity subsitution.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ids"></a><a id="2591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2591" class="Function">ids</a> <a id="2595" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2597" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="2599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2599" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="2600" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2602" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="2610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2599" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2599" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="2614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2591" class="Function">ids</a> <a id="2618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2618" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2620" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2622" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="2624" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2618" class="Bound">x</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The shift operation `↑` constructs the sequence

    1, 2, 3, ...

and is defined as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="↑"></a><a id="2746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2746" class="Function">↑</a> <a id="2748" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2750" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="2752" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2752" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2754" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2754" class="Bound">A</a><a id="2755" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2757" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2759" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="2765" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2752" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2767" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2768" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2752" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2772" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2754" class="Bound">A</a><a id="2773" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="2775" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2746" class="Function">↑</a> <a id="2777" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2777" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2779" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2781" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="2783" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2784" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="2786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2777" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2787" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Given a term `M` and substitution `σ`, the operation
`M • σ` constructs the sequence

    M , σ 0, σ 1, σ 2, ...

This operation is analogous to the `cons` operation of Lisp.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2990" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2997" class="Number">6</a> <a id="2999" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3004" class="Function Operator">_•_</a>

<a id="_•_"></a><a id="3004" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3004" class="Function Operator">_•_</a> <a id="3008" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3010" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="3012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3012" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3014" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3014" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="3016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3016" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3017" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3019" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3021" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3014" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="3024" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3026" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3016" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3027" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3029" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="3037" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3012" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3014" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="3041" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="3049" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3012" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3054" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3016" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3055" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3057" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3014" class="Bound">Δ</a>
<a id="3059" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3060" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3060" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="3062" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3004" class="Function Operator">•</a> <a id="3064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3064" class="Bound">σ</a><a id="3065" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3401" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="3069" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3071" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3060" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="3073" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3074" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3074" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="3076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3004" class="Function Operator">•</a> <a id="3078" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3078" class="Bound">σ</a><a id="3079" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3081" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3082" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="3084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3084" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3085" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3087" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3089" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3078" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="3091" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3084" class="Bound">x</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Given two substitutions `σ` and `τ`, the sequencing operation `σ ⨟ τ`
produces the sequence

    ⟪τ⟫(σ 0), ⟪τ⟫(σ 1), ⟪τ⟫(σ 2), ...
    
That is, it composes the two substitutions by first applying
`σ` and then applying `τ`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3343" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="3350" class="Number">5</a> <a id="3352" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3357" class="Function Operator">_⨟_</a>

<a id="_⨟_"></a><a id="3357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3357" class="Function Operator">_⨟_</a> <a id="3361" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3363" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="3365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3367" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3367" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="3369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3369" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="3370" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3372" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3374" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="3380" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3382" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3367" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="3384" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="3392" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3367" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="3394" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3369" class="Bound">Σ</a> <a id="3396" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3398" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="3404" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3369" class="Bound">Σ</a>
<a id="3408" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3408" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="3410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3357" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="3412" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Bound">τ</a> <a id="3414" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="3418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Bound">τ</a> <a id="3420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="3422" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="3424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3408" class="Bound">σ</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

For the sequencing operation, Abadi et al. use the notation of
function composition, writting `σ ∘ τ`, but still with `σ` applied
before `τ`, which is the opposite of standard mathematical
practice. We instead write `σ ⨟ τ`, because semicolon is
the standard notation for forward function composition.

## The σ algebra equations

The σ algebra includes the following equations.

    (sub-head)  ⟪ M • σ ⟫ (` Z) ≡ M
    (sub-tail)  ↑ ⨟ (M • σ)    ≡ σ
    (sub-η)     (⟪ σ ⟫ (` Z)) • (↑ ⨟ σ) ≡ σ
    (Z-shift)   (` Z) • ↑      ≡ ids
    
    (sub-id)    ⟪ ids ⟫ M      ≡ M
    (sub-app)   ⟪ σ ⟫ (L · M)  ≡ (⟪ σ ⟫ L) · (⟪ σ ⟫ M)
    (sub-abs)   ⟪ σ ⟫ (ƛ N)    ≡ ƛ ⟪ σ ⟫ N
    (sub-sub)   ⟪ τ ⟫ ⟪ σ ⟫ M  ≡ ⟪ σ ⨟ τ ⟫ M

    (sub-idL)   ids ⨟ σ        ≡ σ
    (sub-idR)   σ ⨟ ids        ≡ σ
    (sub-assoc) (σ ⨟ τ) ⨟ θ    ≡ σ ⨟ (τ ⨟ θ)
    (sub-dist)  (M • σ) ⨟ τ    ≡ (⟪ τ ⟫ M) • (σ ⨟ τ)

The first group of equations describe how the `•` operator acts like cons.
The equation `sub-head` says that the variable zero `Z` returns the
head of the sequence (it acts like the `car` of Lisp).  Similarly,
`sub-tail` says that sequencing with shift `↑` returns the tail of the
sequence (it acts like `cdr` of Lisp).  The `sub-η` equation is the
η-expansion rule for sequences, saying that taking the head and tail
of a sequence, and then cons'ing them together yields the original
sequence. The `Z-shift` equation says that cons'ing zero onto the
shifted sequence produces the identity sequence.

The next four equations involve applying substitutions to terms.  The
equation `sub-id` says that the identity substitution returns the term
unchanged. The equations `sub-app` and `sub-abs` says that
substitution is a congruence for the lambda calculus. The `sub-sub`
equation says that the sequence operator `⨟` behaves as intended.

The last four equations concern the sequencing of substitutions.
The first two equations, `sub-idL` and `sub-idR`, say that
`ids` is the left and right unit of the sequencing operator.
The `sub-assoc` equation says that sequencing is associative.
Finally, `sub-dist` says that post-sequencing distributes through cons.

## Relating the σ algebra and subsitution functions

The definitions of substitution `N [ M ]` and parallel subsitution
`subst σ N` depend on several auxiliary functions: `rename`, `exts`,
`ext`, and `subst-zero`. We shall relate those functions to terms in
the σ algebra.


To begin with, renaming can be expressed in terms of substitution.
We have

    rename ρ M ≡ ⟪ ren ρ ⟫ M               (rename-subst-ren)

where `ren` turns a renaming `ρ` into a substitution by post-composing
`ρ` with the identity substitution.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ren"></a><a id="6114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6114" class="Function">ren</a> <a id="6118" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6120" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="6122" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6122" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6124" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6124" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="6125" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6127" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23035" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="6136" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6122" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6138" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6124" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="6140" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6142" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="6148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6122" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6124" class="Bound">Δ</a>
<a id="6152" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6114" class="Function">ren</a> <a id="6156" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6156" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="6158" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2591" class="Function">ids</a> <a id="6164" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="6166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6156" class="Bound">ρ</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

When the renaming is the increment function, then it is equivalent to
shift.

    ren S_ ≡ ↑                           (ren-shift)
    
    rename S_ M ≡ ⟪ ↑ ⟫ M                 (rename-shift)

Next we relate the `exts` function to the σ algebra.  Recall that the
`exts` function extends a substitution as follows:

    exts σ = ` Z, rename S_ (σ 0), rename S_ (σ 1), rename S_ (σ 2), ...

So `exts` is equivalent to cons'ing Z onto the sequence formed
by applying `σ` and then shifting.

    exts σ ≡ ` Z • (σ ⨟ ↑)                (exts-cons-shift)

The `ext` function does the same job as `exts` but for renamings
instead of substitutions. So composing `ext` with `ren` is the same as
composing `ren` with `exts`.

    ren (ext ρ) ≡ exts (ren ρ)            (ren-ext)

Thus, we can recast the `exts-cons-shift` equation in terms of
renamings.

    ren (ext ρ) ≡ ` Z • (ren ρ ⨟ ↑)       (ext-cons-Z-shift)

It is also useful to specialize the `sub-sub` equation of the σ
algebra to the situation where the first substitution is a renaming.

    ⟪ σ ⟫ (rename ρ M) ≡ ⟪ σ ∘ ρ ⟫ M       (rename-subst)

The `subst-zero M` substitution is equivalent to cons'ing
`M` onto the identity substitution.

    subst-zero M ≡ M • ids                (subst-Z-cons-ids)


Finally, sequencing `exts σ` with `subst-zero M` is equivalent to
cons'ing `M` onto `σ`.

    exts σ ⨟ subst-zero M ≡ (M • σ)       (subst-zero-exts-cons)


## Proofs of sub-head, sub-tail, sub-η, Z-shift, sub-idL, sub-dist, and sub-app

We start with the proofs that are immediate from the definitions of
the operators.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sub-tail"></a><a id="7894" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7894" class="Function">sub-tail</a> <a id="7903" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7905" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="7907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7907" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7909" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="7910" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7912" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7913" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7913" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7915" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7915" class="Bound">B</a><a id="7916" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7918" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7919" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7919" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7921" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7909" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="7925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7927" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7913" class="Bound">A</a><a id="7928" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7930" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7931" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7931" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="7933" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7935" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="7941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7907" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#7909" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="7944" class="Symbol">}</a>

## Interlude: congruences

In this section we establish congruence rules for the σ algebra
operators `•` and `⨟` and for `subst` and its helper functions `ext`,
`rename`, `exts`, and `subst-zero`. These congruence rules help with
the equational reasoning in the later sections of this chapter.

[JGS: I would have liked to prove all of these via cong and cong₂,
 but I have not yet found a way to make that work. It seems that
 various implicit parameters get in the way.]

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="cong-ext"></a><a id="9674" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9674" class="Function">cong-ext</a> <a id="9683" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9685" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9687" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9689" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9689" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="9690" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9692" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="9694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9694" class="Bound">ρ′</a> <a id="9697" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23035" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="9706" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9687" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9708" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9689" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="9709" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9711" class="Bound">B</a><a id="9712" class="Symbol">}</a>
   <a id="9717" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9719" class="Symbol">(∀{</a><a id="9722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9722" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9723" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9725" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9692" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="9729" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="9731" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9694" class="Bound">ρ′</a> <a id="9734" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9735" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#9722" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9736" class="Symbol">})</a>

## Relating `rename`, `exts`, `ext`, and `subst-zero` to the σ algebra

In this section we establish equations that relate `subst` and its
helper functions (`rename`, `exts`, `ext`, and `subst-zero`) to terms
in the σ algebra.

The first equation we prove is

    rename ρ M ≡ ⟪ ren ρ ⟫ M              (rename-subst-ren)
               
Because `subst` uses the `exts` function, we need the following lemma
which says that `exts` and `ext` do the same thing except that `ext`
works on renamings and `exts` works on substitutions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ren-ext"></a><a id="13052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13052" class="Function">ren-ext</a> <a id="13060" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13062" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13064" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13065" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="13067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13067" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="13068" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13070" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13070" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13072" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13072" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="13074" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2675" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="13080" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13082" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13083" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="13085" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13087" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23035" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="13094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13065" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="13096" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13067" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="13097" class="Symbol">}</a>

With this lemma in hand, the proof is a straightforward induction on
the term `M`.

  <a id="13861" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
<a id="13863" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13437" class="Function">rename-subst-ren</a> <a id="13880" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13881" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="13883" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13885" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13885" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="13887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="13889" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13889" class="Bound">M</a><a id="13890" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13892" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13894" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1408" class="Function">cong₂</a> <a id="13900" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="13904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13437" class="Function">rename-subst-ren</a> <a id="13921" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13437" class="Function">rename-subst-ren</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The substitution `ren S_` is equivalent to `↑`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ren-shift"></a><a id="14012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14012" class="Function">ren-shift</a> <a id="14022" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14024" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="14026" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14026" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="14027" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14029" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14029" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14030" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14032" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14033" class="Symbol">}</a>
          <a id="14045" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6114" class="Function">ren</a> <a id="14051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a> <a id="14054" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="14056" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2746" class="Function">↑</a> <a id="14058" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14059" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="14061" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14063" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14032" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14064" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14066" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14029" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14068" class="Symbol">}</a>
<a id="14070" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14012" class="Function">ren-shift</a> <a id="14080" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14081" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="14082" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14084" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14085" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14087" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14087" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14088" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14090" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3265" class="Postulate">extensionality</a> <a id="14107" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="14109" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14109" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14111" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14137" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="14119" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14120" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="14122" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14124" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14109" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14125" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="14129" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="14147" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14148" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14150" class="Symbol">:</a> <a The substitution `rename S_ M` is equivalent to shifting: `⟪ ↑ ⟫ M`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="rename-shift"></a><a id="14336" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14336" class="Function">rename-shift</a> <a id="14349" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14351" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="14353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14353" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="14354" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14356" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14357" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14358" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14360" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14361" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14362" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14364" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14365" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="14367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14353" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="14371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="14373" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14357" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14374" class="Symbol">}</a>
             <a id="14389" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14391" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6171" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="14398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a><a id="14401" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14402" class="Argument">B</a> <a id="14404" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14361" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14407" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="14410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14365" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="14412" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="14414" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="14416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2746" class="Function">↑</a> <a id="14418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="14420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14365" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="14422" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14336" class="Function">rename-shift</a><a id="14434" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14435" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14435" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="14436" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14438" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14438" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14439" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14441" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14442" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14444" class="Bound">M</a><a id="14445" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14447" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="14451" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4076" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
    <a id="14461" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6171" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="14468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a> <a id="14471" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14444" class="Bound">M</a>
  <a id="14475" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="14478" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13437" class="Function">rename-subst-ren</a> <a id="14495" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="14501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="14503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6114" class="Function">ren</a> <a id="14507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a> <a id="14510" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="14512" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14444" class="Bound">M</a>

    <a id="14556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="14558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2746" class="Function">↑</a> <a id="14560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="14562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14444" class="Bound">M</a>
  <a id="14566" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Next we prove the equation `exts-cons-shift`, which states that `exts`
is equivalent to cons'ing Z onto the sequence formed by applying `σ`
and then shifting. The proof is by case analysis on the variable `x`,
using `rename-subst-ren` for when `x = S y`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="exts-cons-shift"></a><a id="14849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14849" class="Function">exts-cons-shift</a> <a id="14865" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14867" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="14869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14869" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="14871" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14871" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="14872" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14874" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14875" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14875" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14877" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14877" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14878" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14880" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14881" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14881" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="14883" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14885" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="14891" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14869" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="14893" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14871" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="14894" class="Symbol">}</a>
                <a id="14912" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="14919" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14881" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="14921" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14922" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14875" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14923" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14925" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14877" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14927" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14929" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="14931" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="14934" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3401" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="14936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3004" class="Function Operator">•</a> <a id="14938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14881" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="14941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3357" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="14943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2746" class="Function">↑</a><a id="14944" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="14947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14849" class="Function">exts-cons-shift</a> <a id="14963" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14965" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3265" class="Postulate">extensionality</a> <a id="14980" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="14982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14982" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14984" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14986" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15009" class="Function">lemma</a><a id="14991" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14992" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="14994" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14996" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#14982" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14997" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="15001" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="15009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15009" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="15015" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15017" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="15019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15019" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="15021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link As a corollary, we have a similar correspondence for `ren (ext ρ)`.

  <a id="15532" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Finally, the `subst-zero M` substitution is equivalent to cons'ing `M`
onto the identity substitution.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="subst-Z-cons-ids"></a><a id="15663" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15663" class="Function">subst-Z-cons-ids</a> <a id="15680" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15682" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="15684" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15684" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="15685" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15687" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15689" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15689" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15691" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15693" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2675" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="15697" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15699" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="15701" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15703" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15684" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="15705" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="15707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15689" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15708" class="Symbol">}</a>
                 <a id="15727" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#7359" class="Function">subst-zero</a> <a id="15740" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15699" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="15742" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="15744" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15745" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15699" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="15747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3004" class="Function Operator">•</a> <a id="15749" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2591" class="Function">ids</a><a id="15752" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15754" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15687" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15756" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="15814" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="15822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15822" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="15828" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15830"                       <a id="15895" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#7359" class="Function">subst-zero</a> <a id="15908" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15847" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="15910" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15858" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15912" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="15914" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15915" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15847" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="15917" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3004" class="Function Operator">•</a> <a id="15919" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2591" class="Function">ids</a><a id="15922" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15924" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15858" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="15928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15822" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="15934" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15935" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="15937" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3401" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a><a id="15940" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15942" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15944" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
  <a id="15951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15822" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="15957" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15958" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="15960" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15962" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="15964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15964" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15965" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15967" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15969" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Proofs of sub-abs and sub-id

The equation `sub-abs` follows immediately from the equation
`exts-cons-shift`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sub-abs"></a><a id="16114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16114" class="Function">sub-abs</a> <a id="16122" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16124" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="16126" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16126" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="16128" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16128" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="16129" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16131" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16132" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16132" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="16134" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16136" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="16142" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16126" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="16144" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16128" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="16145" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16147" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16148" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="16150" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16152" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16126" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="16154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16156" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="16158" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="16160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="16161" class="Symbol">}</a>

The proof of `sub-id` requires the following lemma which says that
extending the identity substitution produces the identity
substitution.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="exts-ids"></a><a id="16543" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16543" class="Function">exts-ids</a> <a id="16552" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16554" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="16556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16556" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="16557" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16559" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16559" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16561" class="Bound">B</a><a id="16562" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="16573" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="16580" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2591" class="Function">ids</a> <a id="16584" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="16586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2591" class="Function">ids</a> <a id="16590" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16556" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="16593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16561" class="Bound">B</a><a id="16596" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16598" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16559" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16600" class="Symbol">}</a>
<a id="16602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16543" class="Function">exts-ids</a> <a id="16611" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16612" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="16613" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16615" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16615" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16616" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16618" class="Bound">B</a><a id="16619" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16621" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3265" class="Postulate">extensionality</a> <a id="16638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16652" class="Function">lemma</a>
  <a id="16646" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="16652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16652" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="16658" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16661" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16663" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16612" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="16667" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16618" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="16671" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="16673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16615" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16674" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16676" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16678" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="16683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2591" class="Function">ids</a> <a id="16687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16661" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16689" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="16691" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2591" class="Function">ids</a> <a id="16695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16661" class="Bound">x</a>
        <a id="16705" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16652" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="16711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3401" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="16713" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16715" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
        <a id="16728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16652" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="16734" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16735" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="16737" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#16737" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16738" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16740" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16742" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of `⟪ ids ⟫ M ≡ M` now follows easily by induction on `M`,
using `exts-ids` in the case for `M ≡ ƛ N`.

## Proof of sub-sub

The `sub-sub` equation states that sequenced substitutions `σ ⨟ τ`
are equivalent to first applying `σ` then applying `τ`.

    ⟪ τ ⟫ ⟪ σ ⟫ M  ≡ ⟪ σ ⨟ τ ⟫ M

The proof requires several lemmas. First, we need to prove the
specialization for renaming.

    rename ρ (rename ρ′ M) ≡ rename (ρ ∘ ρ′) M

This in turn requires the following lemma about `ext`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="compose-ext"></a><a id="17932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17932" class="Function">compose-ext</a> <a id="17944"             <a id="18007" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18009" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="18011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18015" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17955" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="18016" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18018" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="18020" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17972" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="18027" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18030" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="18032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18036" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18037" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17955" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="18039" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="18041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17972" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="18043" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18045" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17992" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18047" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18049" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17990" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18051" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="18104" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="18112" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18112" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="18118" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18120"               <a id="18199" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18201" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="18203" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18129" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="18208" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18210" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="18212" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18213" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18217" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18146" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="18219" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18222" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18170" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18224" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="18226" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18230" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18231" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18129" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="18233" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="18235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18146" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="18237" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18239" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18170" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="18243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18112" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="18249" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18250" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="18252" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18254" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3401" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a><a id="18255" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18257" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18259" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
  <a id="18266" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18112" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="18272" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18273" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="18275" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="18279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18279" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18280" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18282" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18284" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

To prove that composing renamings is equivalent to appying one after
the other using `rename`, we proceed by induction on the term `M`,
using the `compose-ext` lemma in the case for `M ≡ ƛ N`.

        <a id="18985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6171" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="18992" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18993" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18997" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18998" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18694" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="19000" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="19002" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18697" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="19004" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18691" class="Bound">N</a>
      <a id="19015" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>        
<a id="19025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18508" class="Function">compose-rename</a> <a id="19040" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19041" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="19043" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19045" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19045" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="19047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="19049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19049" class="Bound">M</a><a id="19050" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19052" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19054" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1408" class="Function">cong₂</a> <a id="19060" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="19064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18508" class="Function">compose-rename</a> <a id="19079" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18508" class="Function">compose-rename</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The next lemma states that if a renaming and subtitution commute on
variables, then they also commute on terms. We explain the proof in
detail below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="commute-subst-rename"></a><a id="19270" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19270" class="Function">commute-subst-rename</a> <a id="19291" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19293" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="19295" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19295" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19297" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="19298" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19300" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19300" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="19302" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19304" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19295" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="19308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="19309" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19311" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19311" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="19313" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19315" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="19321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19295" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19323" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19297" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="19324" class="Symbol">}</a>
                        <a id="19350" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19351" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="19353" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19355" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="19357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19357" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19358" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19360" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#23035" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="19369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19357" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19371" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19372" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19357" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19374" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="19376" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="19377" class="Symbol">)}</a>

       <a id="19892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="19897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19898" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="19903" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19577" class="Bound">σ</a><a id="19904" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="19911" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19580" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="19913" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="19916" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19869" class="Bound">y</a><a id="19917" class="Symbol">))</a>

     <a id="20266" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
<a id="20268" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19270" class="Function">commute-subst-rename</a> <a id="20289" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20290" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="20292" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20294" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20294" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="20296" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="20298" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20298" class="Bound">M</a><a id="20299" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20301" class="Argument">ρ</a> <a id="20303" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20305" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20305" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="20306" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20308" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="20310" class="Symbol">=</a>
   <a id="20315" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1408" class="Function">cong₂</a> <a id="20321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="20325" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20326" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19270" class="Function">commute-subst-rename</a><a id="20346" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20347" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="20349" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20294" class="Bound">L</a><a id="20352" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20354" class="Argument">ρ</a> <a id="20356" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20305" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="20359" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20308" class="Bound">r</a><a id="20362" class="Symbol">)</a>
             <a id="20377" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20378" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19270" class="Function">commute-subst-rename</a><a id="20398" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20399" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="20401" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20403" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20298" class="Bound">M</a><a id="20404" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20406" class="Argument">ρ</a> <a id="20408" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20305" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="20411" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20413" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#20308" class="Bound">r</a><a id="20414" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof is by induction on the term `M`.

* If `M` is a variable, then we use the premise to conclude.

* If `M ≡ ƛ N`, we conclude using the induction hypothesis for
  `N`. However, to use the induction hypothesis, we must show
  that

        exts (exts σ) (ext ρ x) ≡ rename (ext ρ) (exts σ x)

  We prove this equation by cases on x.

    * If `x = Z`, the two sides are equal by definition.

    * If `x = S y`, we obtain the goal by the following equational reasoning.

          exts (exts σ) (ext ρ (S y))
        ≡ rename S_ (exts σ (ρ y)) 
        ≡ rename S_ (rename S_ (σ (ρ y)      (by the premise)
        ≡ rename (ext ρ) (exts σ (S y))      (by compose-rename)
        ≡ rename ((ext ρ) ∘ S_) (σ y)
        ≡ rename (ext ρ) (rename S_ (σ y))   (by compose-rename)
        ≡ rename (ext ρ) (exts σ (S y))

* If `M` is an application, we obtain the goal using the induction
  hypothesis for each subterm.


The last lemma needed to prove `sub-sub` states that the `exts`
function distributes with sequencing. It is a corollary of
`commute-subst-rename`. We describe the proof below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="exts-seq"></a><a id="21541" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21541" class="Function">exts-seq</a> <a id="21550" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21552" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="21554" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21554" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="21556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21556" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="21558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21558" class="Bound">Δ′</a><a id="21560" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21562" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21563" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21563" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="21566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21568" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="21574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21554" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="21576" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21556" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="21577" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21579" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21580" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21580" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="21583" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="21591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21556" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="21593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21558" class="Bound">Δ′</a><a id="21595" class="Symbol">}</a>
   <a id="21600" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21602" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21604" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21605" class="Bound">A</a><a id="21606" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21608" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="21616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21563" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="21619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3357" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="21621" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="21626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21580" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="21628" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21630" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21605" class="Bound">A</a><a id="21632" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21634" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="21636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="21641" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21563" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="21645" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3357" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="21647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21580" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="21649" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="21651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21541" class="Function">exts-seq</a> <a id="21660" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#3265" class="Postulate">extensionality</a> <a id="21677" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="21679" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21679" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21681" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21707" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="21689" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21690" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="21692" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21679" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21695" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="21699" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="21707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21707" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="21713" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21715" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="21717" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21717" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="21719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link
