     <a id="21932" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4134" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
       <a id="21943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="21945" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="21950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21877" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="21953" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="21955" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21956" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6171" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="21963" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a> <a id="21966" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21873" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="21970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21870" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21971" class="Symbol">))</a>

       <a id="22043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6171" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="22050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a> <a id="22053" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22054" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="22056" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21877" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="22059" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="22061" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22062" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21873" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="22065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21870" class="Bound">x</a><a id="22066" class="Symbol">))</a>
     <a id="22074" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4134" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
       <a id="22085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6171" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="22092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a> <a id="22095" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="22097" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21873" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="22100" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3357" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="22102" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21877" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="22104" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21870" class="Bound">x</a><a id="22107" class="Symbol">)</a>
     <a id="22114" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof proceed by cases on `x`.

* If `x = Z`, the two sides are equal by the definition of `exts`
  and sequencing.

* If `x = S x`, we unfold the first use of `exts` and sequencing, then
  apply the lemma `commute-subst-rename`. We conclude by the
  definition of sequencing.


Now we come to the proof of `sub-sub`, which we explain below.

     <a id="22712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="22716" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="22721" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22658" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="22724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="22726" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="22729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="22734" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22654" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="22737" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="22739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22651" class="Bound">N</a><a id="22740" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="22745" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="22748" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1170" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="22753" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="22756" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22757" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22488" class="Function">sub-sub</a><a id="22764" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22765" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="22767" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22651" class="Bound">N</a><a id="22770" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="22772" class="Argument">σ₁</a> <a id="22775" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22777" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="22782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22654" class="Bound">σ₁</a><a id="22784" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="22786" class="Argument">σ₂</a> <a id="22789" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22791" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="22796" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22658" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="22798" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="22801" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="22808" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22810" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="22812" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="22817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22654" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="22820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3357" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="22822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="22827" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22658" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="22830" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="22832" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22651" class="Bound">N</a>
   <a id="22837" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="22840" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1170" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="22845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="22848" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#10856" class="Function">cong-sub</a><a id="22857" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22858" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="22860" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22651" class="Bound">N</a><a id="22863" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22865" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="22868" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22869" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22870" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22872" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#21541" class="Function">exts-seq</a><a id="22882" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22884" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="22888" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22890" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="22897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22899" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="22901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6623" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="22906" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22908" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22654" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="22911" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#3357" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="22913" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22658" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="22915" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22917" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="22919" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22651" class="Bound">N</a>
   <a id="22924" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
<a id="22926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22488" class="Function">sub-sub</a> <a id="22934" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22935" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="22937" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22939" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="22941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="22943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22943" class="Bound">M</a><a id="22944" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22946" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22948" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1408" class="Function">cong₂</a> <a id="22954" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="22958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22959" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22488" class="Function">sub-sub</a><a id="22966" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22967" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="22969" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22971" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22939" class="Bound">L</a><a id="22972" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="22975" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22488" class="Function">sub-sub</a><a id="22983" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22984" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="22986" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22943" class="Bound">M</a><a id="22989" class="Symbol">})</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We proceed by induction on the term `M`.

* If `M = x`, then both sides are equal to `σ₂ (σ₁ x)`.

* If `M = ƛ N`, we first use the induction hypothesis to show that 

     ƛ ⟪ exts σ₂ ⟫ (⟪ exts σ₁ ⟫ N) ≡ ƛ ⟪ exts σ₁ ⨟ exts σ₂ ⟫ N

  and then use the lemma `exts-seq` to show

    ƛ ⟪ exts σ₁ ⨟ exts σ₂ ⟫ N ≡ ƛ ⟪ exts ( σ₁ ⨟ σ₂) ⟫ N

* If `M` is an application, we use the induction hypothesis
  for both subterms.


The following corollary of `sub-sub` specializes the first
substitution to a renaming.

## Proof of sub-assoc

The proof of `sub-assoc` follows directly from `sub-sub` and the
definition of sequencing.

## Proof of subst-zero-exts-cons

The last equation we needed to prove `subst-zero-exts-cons` was
`sub-assoc`, so we can now go ahead with its proof.  We simply apply
the equations for `exts` and `subst-zero` and then apply the σ algebra
equation to arrive at the normal form `M • σ`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="subst-zero-exts-cons"></a><a id="24761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24761" class="Function">subst-zero-exts-cons</a> <a id="24782" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24784" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24786" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24788" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24788" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="24789" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24791" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24791" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="24793" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="24801" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24786" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24803" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24788" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="24804" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24806" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24806" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24807" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24809" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="24811" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24788" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="24815" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="24817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24806" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24818" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24820" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24821" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="25417" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Proof of the substitution lemma

We first prove the generalized form of the substitution lemma, showing
that a substitution `σ` commutes with the subusitution of `M` into
`N`.

    ⟪ exts σ ⟫ N [ ⟪ σ ⟫ M ] ≡ ⟪ σ ⟫ (N [ M ])

This proof is where the σ algebra pays off.  The proof is by direct
equational reasoning. Starting with the left-hand side, we apply σ
algebra equations, oriented left-to-right, until we arive at the
normal form

    ⟪ ⟪ σ ⟫ M • σ ⟫ N

We then do the same with the right-hand side, arriving at the same
normal form. 

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="subst-commute"></a><a id="25991" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#25991" class="Function">subst-commute</a> <a id="26005" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26007" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="26009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26009" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26014" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="26016" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26009" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26020" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="26022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="26024" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150"      <a id="27202" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="27205" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1170" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="27210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="27212" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26132" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="27214" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="27216" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27217" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#838" class="Function">sym</a> <a id="27221" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27222" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#10856" class="Function">cong-sub</a><a id="27230" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27231" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="27233" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26126" class="Bound">N</a><a id="27236" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27238" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#15663" class="Function">subst-Z-cons-ids</a> <a id="27255" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="27259" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="27262" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
       <a id="27271" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="27273" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26132" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="27275" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2076" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="27277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27278" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26126" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="27280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#7475" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="27282" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26129" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="27284" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#7475" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="27285" class="Symbol">)</a>
     <a id="27292" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

A corollary of `subst-commute` is that `rename` also commutes with
substitution. In the proof below, we first exchange `rename ρ` for
the substitution `⟪ ren ρ ⟫`, and apply `subst-commute`, and
then convert back to `rename ρ`.

     <a id="28086" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="28089" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#838" class="Function">sym</a> <a id="28093" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#13437" class="Function">rename-subst-ren</a><a id="28110" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28112" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4193" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
       <a id="28121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6171" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="28128" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#27716" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="28130" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28131" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#27710" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="28133" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#7475" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="28135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#27713" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="28137" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#7475" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="28138" class="Symbol">)</a>
     <a id="28145" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

To present the substitution lemma, we introduce the following notation
for substituting a term `M` for index 1 within term `N`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_〔_〕"></a><a id="28301" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28301" class="Function Operator">_〔_〕</a> <a id="28306" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28308" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="28310" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28311" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28311" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28313" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28313" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28315" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28315" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28317" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28317" class="Bound">C</a><a id="28318" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="28328" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28330" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28311" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28332" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28334" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28315" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28336" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28338" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28317" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="28340" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="28342" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28313" class="Bound">A</a>

The substitution lemma is stated as follows and proved as a corollary
of the `subst-commute` lemma.

## Notes

Most of the properties and proofs in this file are based on the paper
_Autosubst: Reasoning with de Bruijn Terms and Parallel Substitution_
by Schafer, Tebbi, and Smolka (ITP 2015). That paper, in turn, is
based on the paper of Abadi, Cardelli, Curien, and Levy (1991) that
defines the σ algebra.


## Unicode

This chapter uses the following unicode:
    ⟪  U+27EA  MATHEMATICAL LEFT DOUBLE ANGLE BRACKET (\<<)
    ⟫  U+27EA  MATHEMATICAL RIGHT DOUBLE ANGLE BRACKET (\>>)
    ↑  U+2191  UPWARDS ARROW (\u)
    •  U+2022  BULLET (\bub)
    ⨟  U+2A1F  Z NOTATION SCHEMA COMPOSITION (C-x 8 RET Z NOTATION SCHEMA COMPOSITION)
    〔  U+3014  LEFT TORTOISE SHELL BRACKET (\( option 9 on page 2)
    〕  U+3015  RIGHT TORTOISE SHELL BRACKET (\) option 9 on page 2)
